		<div class="wpb_wrapper" id="ct_anij22bdg0qexuba1b9c">
			<p style="text-align: center;">Student Care Anchorvale | Singapore | PlayFACTO School Anchorvale</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">Re-discover The Future &amp; Fun of Learning</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">PlayFACTO School Anchorvale was conceptualised to meet working families’ demand for premium and reliable student care services.</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">Our unique Positive Education approach and vibrant Reggio-inspired learning environment provide students with engaging experiences that develop them holistically, balancing between academic excellence and social-emotional learning, equipping our students with the essential skills to overcome the challenges of today and navigate the uncertainties of tomorrow, all within a home-like environment.</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">Students are encouraged to discover and develop their interests and creativity, learn critical soft skills, acquire positive attitudes and enhance their social interactions with peers.</p>

		<div class="wpb_wrapper" id="ct_0rrjtd9qse0zg72nv4ei">
			<p>Student Care Anchorvale: PlayFACTO School was started to provide quality education service with a positive focus. We are the first and only Positive Education Student Care &amp; Enrichment Brand in Singapore accredited by PESA (Positive Education School Association).</p>
<p>We bring together the science of positive psychology with best-practice teaching. PlayFACTO School is a place where students (both student care &amp; enrichment) cultivate their intellectual minds and develop a broad set of character strengths, virtues, life skills, and competencies, which support their well-being and prepare them for the challenges in the 21<sup>st</sup> century.</p>
<p>At Student Care Anchorvale, PlayFACTO School, we adopt a whole-school approach to embrace Positive Education and deliver a ‘fun’ learning experience. All teachers and support staff participate in training programs to acquire Positive Education tools that they can apply in their work and personal lives. For students at PlayFACTO School, Positive Education is incorporated into our student care &amp; STEAM enrichment curriculum.</p>

		</div>
